  >

  > 
  > Feel 20kg Lighter:
  > Experience up to 20kg of effortless lifting power whenever you stand up, climb stairs, or squat. Every upward motion feels lighter, smoother, and easier than ever.
  > 
  > Self-Evolving AI for Personalized Support:
  > The Z1’s intelligent system learns and adapts to you for seamless, natural assistance — every step, climb, or descent.
  >

  > Only 680g. Lightweight, ergonomic design for all-day wear with no bulk.

## 9. Randonnée sans douleur ? Mon test de l’exosquelette DNsys Z1

- **频道：** La tanière de JR
- **观看数：** 19,440
- **点赞数：** 424
- **评论数：** 121
- **时长：** 10:01
- **发布日期：** 2025-08-11T15:30:21Z
- **链接：** https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=PY9rxf6V1gw
- **来源：** search
- **有字幕：** 否
- **语言：** fr
- **缩略图：** https://i.ytimg.com/vi/PY9rxf6V1gw/hqdefault.jpg
- **简介：**

  > 🔗 Plus d’infos et campagne Kickstarter : https://dada.link/lW73Mx
  > J’ai voulu savoir si cet exosquelette apportait vraiment quelque chose…
  > Pour ça, j’ai fait un test très simple : un parcours complet sans le DNsys Z1, puis exactement le même avec.
  > 
  > En montée, on sent clairement l’assistance : l’effort est toujours là, mais l’appareil vous aide à économiser de l’énergie, un peu comme un vélo à assistance électrique par rapport à un vélo classique.
  > En descente, l’effet est encore plus marquant : il freine vos mouvements, réduit l’impact sur les genoux et les articulations, et apporte une vraie sensation de sécurité. Pour quelqu’un qui revient d’une blessure ou qui a un peu d’appréhension dans les pentes, ce maintien supplémentaire peut vraiment redonner confiance.
  > 
  > Ce n’est pas un gadget : la sensation de soutien est bien réelle, et sur de longues randos, ça peut faire une grosse différence.
  > 
  > 📅 Sortie prévue : automne 2025
  >

## 16. My FIRST Exoskeleton Legs Are...(DNSYS Z1)

- **频道：** CKid
- **观看数：** 25,007

## 20. I TESTED the Dnsys Z1 &amp; X1 Exoskeleton at CES 2026 *Im Superhuman Now*

- **频道：** ManShed
- **观看数：** 10,394
- **点赞数：** 222
- **评论数：** 8
- **时长：** 6:20
- **发布日期：** 2026-01-19T19:16:04Z
- **链接：** https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=cIGlR-PddxQ
- **来源：** search
- **有字幕：** 否
- **语言：** en
- **缩略图：** https://i.ytimg.com/vi/cIGlR-PddxQ/hqdefault.jpg
- **简介：**

  > 👇 Check the links below for more details
  > 
  > Z1:https://dada.link/RjWhIn
  > X1：https://dada.link/LLRhq0
  > Dnsys channel: @DnsysTech
  > #Dnsys #Exoskeleton #AIexoskeleton
  > 
  > Walking uphill, downhill, or carrying heavy gear doesn’t have to destroy your knees anymore. In this video, I’m taking a real-world look at the Dnsys Z1 knee exoskeleton, paired with the X1 base, and breaking down what it actually feels like to use wearable mobility tech designed to support your movement—not replace it.
  > 
  > The Z1 delivers up to 50% intelligent power assist, helping reduce up to 35kg of load when walking, climbing, or tackling uneven terrain. One of the most impressive features is downhill support—where the system acts like an invisible stool, reducing knee pressure by up to 200% for safer, more stable descents.
  > 
  > What really sets this apart is how natural it feels. Weighing just 680 grams, the Z1 is currently the lightest knee exoskeleton available, yet it’s powered by a 900W DNA-1 motor that delivers smooth, precise motion with lower resistance and higher torque accuracy. Add in advanced AI that recognizes your movement in 0.01 seconds and learns your gait over time, and the experience feels surprisingly intuitive.
  > 
  > Battery life is just as practical, with up to 25 km of range, regenerative charging while walking downhill, and USB-C fast charging that gets you 20% battery in only 8 minutes.
  > 
  > If you’re curious about wearable tech, exoskeletons, or how AI-powered mobility can reduce fatigue and joint strain, this video is worth checking out.
  > 
  > 👍 Like, subscribe, and let me know—where would you use something like this?
  > 
  > #DnsysZ1 #WearableTech #MobilityTech #AI #FutureTech #KneeSupport #HikingGear #TechReview #ces2026

## 23. 外骨骼專題 08：2025年消費級外骨骼產業盤點：DNSYS Z1延遲發貨、死亡擱淺2聯名版、韓國針對兒童的外骨骼、ACENTIZ模組化外骨骼總整理

- **频道：** RIDER 睿德智趣
- **观看数：** 1,292
- **点赞数：** 0
- **评论数：** 9
- **时长：** 18:36
- **发布日期：** 2025-12-29T14:00:06Z
- **链接：** https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=oZxF6DNnoE4
- **来源：** search
- **有字幕：** 是
- **语言：** zh-TW
- **缩略图：** https://i.ytimg.com/vi/oZxF6DNnoE4/hqdefault.jpg
- **简介：**

  > ※以下是影片總結懶人包：
  > 
  > 2025外骨骼產業最新發展狀況總結
  > 
  > 1. 外骨骼產品現況與市場動態
  > • 外骨骼技術持續快速進步，近期有多項新產品與合作消息。
  > • 消費級外骨骼市場競爭激烈，以中國大陸與韓國品牌為主，美國及其他國家品牌較少。
  > 2. 主要品牌與產品進展
  > DNSYS Z1 膝關節外骨骼
  > • 於Kickstarter眾籌，原預計11月中發貨，現延至12月中，部分贊助者可能需等至明年初。
  > • 軍方及年輕族群對膝關節外骨骼需求大，因操練導致膝關節損傷普遍。
  > • DNSYS與遊戲《死亡擱淺2》聯名推出特別版，價格高達1998美金，市場定位與實際需求族群存在落差。
  > WI ROBOTIC 韓國品牌
  > • 推出髖關節外骨骼，主打韓國設計製造，價格約台幣6.3萬元，較同類產品高。
  > • 新發展聚焦兒童市場，產品可隨兒童成長調整，鎖定行動障礙兒童，預計2026年或2027年量產。
  > ASCENTIZ（程天科技）模組化外骨骼
  > • 產品以腰帶為核心，可切換髖關節（H模組）或膝關節（K模組）。
  > • 目前僅能二選一，無法同時支援兩種關節，屬於消費級產品初步嘗試。
  > • 公司背景為中國大陸醫療型下肢機器人廠商，首次進軍消費市場，市場反應待觀察。
  > 其他國際品牌
  > • 美國SKIP與始祖鳥合作推出膝關節外骨骼褲，預計明年發貨，定價4999美金，採預購制，量產規模有限，市場接受度待考驗。
  > 3. 市場需求與用戶觀察
  > • 行動不便族群對外骨骼產品需求強烈，尤其是膝關節與髖關節輔助。
  > • 兒童行動障礙市場逐漸受到關注，產品數量有限但具有社會意義。
  > • 消費級外骨骼目前無法幫助完全無法行走者，適合有部分行走能力者使用。
  > 4. 產業趨勢與展望
  > • 消費級外骨骼預計於2025至2027年間進入爆發成長期。
  > • 技術進步與市場競爭將帶動產品功能提升與價格下降。
  > • 全球人口老化趨勢帶動外骨骼需求，期望台灣及其他國家廠商積極投入研發及零組件生產。
  > 5. 結語
  > • 外骨骼產業持續進步，新產品與新市場不斷出現，值得持續關注。
  > • 有興趣者可透過Facebook、YouTube或實體店面與官方聯絡，獲取最新資訊。
  > 
  > #外骨骼 #登山體驗 #VIGX #智慧助行 #金面山 #RIDER #外骨骼科技 #DNSYS #創業觀察 #行動輔助 #健走科技  #肯綮 #hypershell #VIGX #動力外骨骼 #行走輔助 #登山裝備 #輔助行走 #爬山神器
  > 
  > ※睿德智趣有限公司 Rider Techjoy Co., Ltd.
  > ​RIDER 專注於個人移動領域，自2014年成立以來，我們發現並代理各式優質的個人移動產品，並提供完善的售後服務。
  > 
  > 公司地址：台北市士林區延平北路五段302巷36號
  > RIDER 官網：https://www.rider.cool
  > RIDER 商城：https://www.riderstore.tw
  > TEL : (02) 2813-6996
  > ​營業時間：11:00~20:00 (周日&周一公休) 
  > 服務信箱 :  service@rider.cool

## 36. Lightweight and accesible! Chinese exoskeletons shine at CES 2026

- **频道：** ShanghaiEye魔都眼
- **观看数：** 154,358
- **点赞数：** 1,699
- **评论数：** 516
- **时长：** 2:11
- **发布日期：** 2026-01-10T11:00:32Z
- **链接：** https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=E8qlqAe62pk
- **来源：** search
- **有字幕：** 否
- **语言：** en
- **缩略图：** https://i.ytimg.com/vi/E8qlqAe62pk/hqdefault.jpg
- **标签：** Shanghai, Shanghaieye, Dragon TV, 上海, 东方卫视, Shanghai TV, 魔都眼, 魔都, Shanghai Media Group, Dnsys, Dynamic Network Systems, CES 2026, Dnsys Z1, Ascentiz, Ascentiz-H, Ascentiz-K, Las Vegas, United States, Chinese startups
- **简介：**

  > Shenzhen-based technology startup Dnsys (Dynamic Network Systems) showcased its latest products at CES 2026.
  > 
  > The Dnsys Z1 is a lightweight, consumer-focused robotic exoskeleton designed to make walking, hiking, and running easier and more efficient. 
  > 
  > The Z1 knee exoskeleton does offers a 50% boost in the wearer's calf and thigh strength while reducing knee pressure by 200%.
  > 
  > It is positioned as a personal mobility enhancer for outdoor enthusiasts and active individuals.
  > 
  > Ascentiz, another Chinese startup in wearable robotics, introduced its groundbreaking modular exoskeleton system. 
  > 
  > The Ascentiz platform—comprising the hip module (Ascentiz-H) and knee module (Ascentiz-K)—leverages two distinct drive technologies optimized for the biomechanical demands of each joint, delivering intuitive and powerful movement support for dynamic and load-bearing activities.
  > 
  > One of the obstacles to overcome is the idea that exoskeletons reduce physical effort and diminish the health benefits of exercise.
  >

- **热门评论（39 条）：**

  > **@ottoHerdegen** [👍27]：Vielen Dank Riko für die Vorstellung dieses Gerätes. Ich bin 69 und  wie du es im Video nennst bewegungsreduziert. Auf ebener Strecke schaffe ich gerade mal ca. 200-500m, je nach Tagesform. Ursache ist eine Hemiparese (halbseitige Lähmung) nach einem Schlaganfall. Das Gerät, oder genauergesagt natürlich die Geräte, scheinen eine echte Hilfe zu sein, z.B. auch nach einer Knie-OP. Ganz allgemein gesagt: Bewegungsprobleme haben immer einen Anfang, und oftmals auch ein Ende. wer die Möglichkeit hat, für seine Gesundheit/Bewegungsfähigkeit zu behalten, oder gar wieder zu steigern, der sollte dies tun. Es ist nicht schön, wenn die erreichbaren Fotospots immer näher rücken, und man irgendwann mit jedem Stein, jedem Tier und jeder Pflanze in Sichtweite/Reichweite per du ist. Da macht selbst fotografieren keinen Spass mehr. Kurz gesagt: tut was für eure Gesundheit, ihr habt nur eine! Darum auch an dich Riko ein großes Dankeschön für die Vorstellung und dieses Video! Es zeigt mir, dass du an mehr interessiert bist, als an Klicks.<br>PS: Nachdem ich einige Kommentare gelesen habe möchte ich ergänzen: Ich finde es total daneben, wenn sich gesunde Menschen über Hilfen/Hilfsgeräte lustig machen, die kranken und behinderten Menschen einen Teil ihrer Lebensqualität zurück geben können!!!

Kein Leistungssport (der belastet am Ende auch nur), sondern sorgt für ausreichend GESUNDE Bewegung, solange ihr noch schmerzfrei seid. Das kann sich nämlich schlagmals ändern und dies tritt um so eher ein, je weniger ihr Euch bewegt. Und dann, ja dann braucht ihr plötzlich so ein Hilfsmittel. Tut lieber jetzt etwas für Euch. Auch ich habe geglaubt, &quot;unzerstörbar&quot; zu sein und es bitter bereut...

## 41. Best Exoskeleton for Outdoor Adventure?

- **频道：** Grim Granite
- **观看数：** 1,258
- **点赞数：** 37
- **评论数：** 16
- **时长：** 7:49
- **发布日期：** 2026-01-27T16:23:58Z
- **链接：** https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=Nz3xd4VoynA
- **来源：** search
- **有字幕：** 否
- **语言：** en-US
- **缩略图：** https://i.ytimg.com/vi/Nz3xd4VoynA/hqdefault.jpg
- **简介：**

  > What if the future of hiking isn’t lighter gear… but stronger legs?
  > 
  > At CES, the world’s largest technology expo, I tried something I never expected to see outside of science fiction: real, working exoskeletons designed for everyday people — and for the trail.
  > Check out the @dnsys.ai units here:  https://dada.link/xK9tOv  https://dada.link/yWjkQ5
  > 
  > In this video, I test two hiking-focused exoskeletons from Dnsys:
  > 
  > • The X1 Hip Exoskeleton, built to assist your stride and reduce fatigue on long walks and hikes
  > • The Z1 Knee Exoskeleton, the world’s first of its kind, designed to protect your knees, add power to each step, and make climbing and descents easier
  > 
  > I also talk with Dnsys COO & co-founder Jojo to talk about why they built these devices, how they work, and their mission to help people stay active, independent, and connected to nature.
  > 
  > With over 10,000 X1 units already in use and the Z1 currently breaking records in crowdfunding, this technology may represent a true “physical revolution” — changing how far we can hike, how long we can explore, and who gets to keep adventuring outdoors.
  > 
  > We also talk about:
  > 
  > • How the Z1 learns your movement patterns in real time
  > • How it redistributes load to reduce knee strain
  > • Why it can make users feel dramatically lighter while hiking
  > • The Death Stranding collaboration and the philosophy of connecting humans, technology, and nature
  > 
  > As someone with multiple knee surgeries, I was especially curious whether this kind of tech could actually make a difference on the trail — and the results surprised me.
  > 
  > Would you hike with an exoskeleton?
  > 
  > Let me know in the comments, and thanks for watching. I’ll see you out there. 🏔️🥾
  > #Dnsys #exoskeleton #AIexoskeleton

## 45. How to use the DNSYS X1?

- **频道：** DNSYS
- **观看数：** 3,197
- **点赞数：** 36
- **评论数：** 13
- **时长：** 2:20
- **发布日期：** 2024-12-02T11:38:10Z
- **链接：** https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=dtaYg2uVRqg
- **来源：** channel
- **有字幕：** 否
- **语言：** en
- **缩略图：** https://i.ytimg.com/vi/dtaYg2uVRqg/hqdefault.jpg
- **简介：**

  > This video will provide a quick guide on how to correctly wear the DNSYS X1. Please read the instruction manual before using the DNSYS X1, and follow the beginner's tutorial in the app.
  > 
  > Please note: After turning it on, please quickly double-tap the power button. When the breathing light starts flashing, pressing the + or - buttons on either side will enter working mode. Eco, Sport, and Boost provide assistance. Aqua and Aqua+ provide resistance.
  > 
  > Thank you for following these guidelines.

- **热门评论（5 条）：**

  > **@KarmicStuff** [👍2]：Sorry, this is not well done at all.  First, solve the annoying excessive soundtrack by muting.  Every production by this company seems to say &#39;refer to manual&#39;; manual says, &#39;refer to instructions&#39;, etc.  Referred everywhere, including on their website, and you will not find any written description of HOW TO USE the damned thing!  Not how to put it on.  Not how to charge it.  This poor excuse for an instructional video does show the pushing of buttons, done too quickly and far too closely to the subject to have perspective regarding what button is being pushed.  Generally, if the unit is cooperating, the unit ASSIST button is the right side button.  You get 2 lights and a tone after pushing is once, giving you level one (why 2 lights when it should have been one?)),  Push the R button again for the next ASSIST level (Sport), you expect to see it change to 3 lights but it doesn&#39;t, stays on 2 - but the beep tone sounds a little different.  Press that R button a third time, you get the 3rd, highest ASSIST (Boost) level - but you do NOT get yellow lights as shown in the video.  Instead, you get two bright RED LED lights showing the highest setting of ASSIST.  (The RESISTANCE levels are L side button activated, less likely to be used, generally similar to ASSIST side in reverse)<br>     Half of the time nothing happens when you press side buttons after the double click on the power button, awkwardly located at the middle of your back for unknown design reasons.  Others have reported confusion with how to turn it on and make it work correctly.  There is a learning curve involved in figuring it out and finding some rhythm.  It is an interesting, new product that will probably be quickly improved.  It may be somewhat overpriced currently, given startup issues; the value proposition should increase over time given normal markets.<br>In other words, it might be worth waiting awhile before spending $1000 or so on any variation of this product.  It is nowhere near the value of e-bikes at current prices.
  >
  > **@Mattbriggs85** [👍1]：Well done, this looks improved. Next interaction one that can be worn under clothes
  >
  > **@amyleveridge8589** [👍1]：instructions suck!! we can&#39;t get it to work
  >

- **来源：** channel
- **有字幕：** 否
- **语言：** en
- **缩略图：** https://i.ytimg.com/vi/0RxyZRyELa0/hqdefault.jpg
- **简介：**

  > For the most comfortable and effective use of the DNSYS X1:
  > 
  > Position the waist belt 3–5 cm below your belly button.
  > Adjust the leg plates so they sit 3–5 cm above your knees.
  > Make sure both motors remain parallel to each other for optimal power and assistance.
